 Saying that the situation would have been better had it not been spent on import of coal and if we had extracted our own coal
 magar jab jetali vitt mantri bane or piyush goly koyala mantri tab kya kuch badal gaya, kyonki aaj bhi rupee kii keemat girti ja rahi he or vittiya ghate par dabaav bad rahaa he
 In the 'business Standard' dated May 17, 2018, Jayjit Das wrote that in 2017-18, 213 million tonnes of coal were imported, an increase of 8 percent from the previous year and it cost $ 22 billion
 yani jo sthiti 2013 main thi vahi 2017 main bhi rahi
 Politics does not change with this kind of research, it moves with deception and misleading
 manmohan singh ne pradhanmantri ke taur par jetali kii maang kaa jawaab bhi diya tha 30 agast 2013 ko
 See what a coincidence
 desh ke baahar kuch apratyaashit ghatnaon se bazaar par vipareet pratikriya hui he, jiske kaaran rupee kii keemat main tezi se giravat ai

 isse ubhartee hui arthvyavasthaaon main puunji ke pravaah par vipareet prabhaav padaa, jiske kaaran na sirf rupee main balki brazil kii riyal, turki kii lira, indonesia ke rupia, dakshin africa ke rand or anya mudraon main bhi tezi se giravat aa rahi he

 Increasing the power of corruption and brightening it means becoming institutionalized
 bhrashtachar kii badhati sookshmata puri duniya main sabase badi chunauti he, ladaai isliye kathin hoti ja rahi he ki jab tak log bhrashtachar ko samajhakar or jaagruk hokar yaa iske viruddh lamaband ho pate hai, tab tak yah sansthagat ho jaataa he

 The controversial Gujkok (gujarat Terrorism and Organized Crime Prevention Act, gujcotoca) bill in Gujarat has got the approval of the Governor
 gujarat vidhansabha main virodh ke bich yah bill 30 march ko chauthi baar paas hua tha
 Since then, many organizations in Gujarat are opposing it
 ye sanghathan apni baat kehane ke liye 18 april ko rajyapal se mili the or is bill ko naamanzoor karne kii unase guzarish kii thi
 But, now news is coming that the Governor has stamped his approval on this bill and sent it to the Ministry of Home Affairs for the President's approval
 ye bill dobaaraa se ab raashtrapati ke paas pahunchaa he, mahatvapurn he ki isse pehle do raashtrapati is bill ke aapattijanak praavdhaanon ke chalate is bill ko naamanzoor kar chuke hai
 The provisions of this bill, which are opposed, are that the statement made in front of the police can be considered as evidence and it can also be presented in the court as evidence, the period of police remand is generally up to 15 days
 It can be up to 30 days in cases filed under it
 saath hi kisi maamle main chargeshit daayar karne kii samaysima jo aam taur par 90 dinon kii hoti he, use badhaakar 180 din kii ja rahi he
 The protesting Congress and the human rights activists fear that these provisions will bring considerable power to the police, which is likely to be misused

 bajet main arun jetali gold diposit acount kholane kaa elaan kiya he
 This means that if you have gold in your house, you can deposit it in the bank and get interest on its value
 bilkul vaise jaise aap bank main paisa jamaakar byaaj pate hai

 kahaan par khulenge gold monetigeshan account?gold acount general bainkon main hi khulenge, jahaan par loker kii suvidha ho
